				<div class="article-body">

					<figure class="alignnone img-container shareable-item" style="max-width:620px"><div class="img-wrap">
<a id="item-0" class="anchor"></a><div class="item-share-buttons item-share">
<a class="share-item share-item-facebook btn" title="Share this on Facebook" data-track="share-item-facebook"><span class="icon icon-facebook"></span></a><a class="share-item share-item-twitter btn" target="_blank" title="Share this on Twitter" data-track="share-item-twitter" rel="noopener"><span class="icon icon-twitter"></span></a><a class="share-item share-item-pinterest btn" target="_blank" title="Share this on Pinterest" data-track="share-item-pinterest" rel="noopener"><span class="icon icon-pinterest"></span></a>
</div>
<img data-orig-id="7400797" data-orig-w="1024" data-orig-h="682" data-max-width="748" width="748" height="498" data-rsz="shrink" src="https://metrouk2.files.wordpress.com/2018/03/sei_3881307.jpg?w=748&amp;h=498&amp;crop=1" alt="Former French president Nicolas Sarkozy arrested and in police custody" class="img-align-none size-full wp-image-7400797" data-rewritten="true">
</div>
<figcaption>Nicolas Sarkozy is answering questions at a police station in Nanterre over irregularities in campaign funding (Picture: Reuters)</figcaption></figure><p>Former French President Nicolas Sarkozy is in police custody over allegations he received funds from late Libyan dictator Colonel Gaddafi.</p>
<p>The questions relate to the financing of his 2007 presidential campaign, which he won, according to Le Monde.</p>
<a href="http://metro.co.uk/2018/03/20/man-died-colleague-put-air-hose-bottom-switched-7403461/" data-track="in-content-link/1/thumbnail/auto-cat/" data-track-destination="7403461" class="thumbnail-link"><img src="https://metrouk2.files.wordpress.com/2018/03/sei_3970491.jpg?quality=80&amp;strip=all&amp;crop=180px%2C0px%2C842px%2C630px&amp;resize=150%2C113&amp;w=100&amp;h=75" data-aspect="1.3274336283186" alt="Man died when colleague put air hose in his bottom and switched it on" class="thumbnail-link-image" data-rewritten="false"><span class="mor-title">Man died when colleague put air hose in his bottom and switched it on</span></a><p>A former minister and close ally of Sarkozy, Brice Hortefeux, was also being questioned by police on Tuesday morning in relation to the Libya investigation, another source close to the probe said.</p>
<p>Sarkozy, who served as president from 2007 to 2012, has always denied receiving any illicit campaign funding and has dismissed the Libyan allegations as ‘grotesque’.</p>
<p>In January French businessman Alexandre Djouhri, suspected by investigators of funnelling money from Gaddafi to finance Sarkozy’s campaign, was arrested in Britain and granted bail after he appeared in a London court.</p>
<figure class="alignnone img-container shareable-item" style="max-width:620px"><div class="img-wrap">
<a id="item-0" class="anchor"></a><div class="item-share-buttons item-share">
<a class="share-item share-item-facebook btn" title="Share this on Facebook" data-track="share-item-facebook"><span class="icon icon-facebook"></span></a><a class="share-item share-item-twitter btn" target="_blank" title="Share this on Twitter" data-track="share-item-twitter" rel="noopener"><span class="icon icon-twitter"></span></a><a class="share-item share-item-pinterest btn" target="_blank" title="Share this on Pinterest" data-track="share-item-pinterest" rel="noopener"><span class="icon icon-pinterest"></span></a>
</div>
<img data-orig-id="7401046" data-orig-w="1024" data-orig-h="716" data-max-width="620" width="620" height="433" data-rsz="shrink" src="data:image/gif;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mP8/B8AAusB9FD6Pn0AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" data-src="https://metrouk2.files.wordpress.com/2018/03/sei_3888855.jpg?w=620&amp;h=433&amp;crop=1" alt="Tripoli, LYBIA: French President Nicolas Sarkozy (L) is welcomed by Libyan leader Moamer Kadhafi (R) upon his arrival in Tripoli 25 July 2007. Sarkozy arrived in Tripoli for a meeting with Libyan leader Moamer Kadhafi, a day after the release of six foreign medics, an AFP correspondent said. Sarkozy has touted his visit as a &quot;political trip&quot; to help Libya's reintegration into the international community after decades of sanctions and isolation. AFP PHOTO PATRICK KOVARIK (Photo credit should read PATRICK KOVARIK/AFP/Getty Images)" class="img-align-none size-full wp-image-7401046" data-rewritten="true">
</div>
<figcaption>He is being questioned by police in relation to financing from Libya (Picture: Getty)</figcaption></figure><p>Sarkozy has already been ordered to stand trial in a separate matter concerning financing of his failed re-election campaign in 2012, when he was defeated by Francois Hollande.</p>
<div class="ad-slot-container"><div class="ad-slot ad-slot-small ad-slot-in-content" id="mpu_mobile_top"><script>if(window.adverts) { adverts.addToArray({"pos": "mpu_mobile_top"}) }</script></div></div><div class="ad-slot-container"><div class="ad-slot ad-slot-medium ad-slot-in-content" id="mpu_tablet"><script>if(window.adverts) { adverts.addToArray({"pos": "mpu_tablet"}) }</script></div></div><p>He can be held by police for up to 48 hours before facing magistrates.</p>
<p>Elin Jones, the Assembly Member for Ceredigion, posted on Twitter: ‘Awful news in Cardigan. A young, innocent life taken so tragically.</p>
<p>‘Thank you to those who tried to save her, and our thoughts are with all who loved her. Colled ifanc sy’n tristau cymuned. R.I.P Kiara Moore.’</p>

(m = new Image, q.ns_p || (ns_p = m), m.src = a) : c.write("<", "p", "><", 'img src="', a, '" height="1" width="1" alt="*"', "><", "/p", ">")
			},

			trackPageView: function () {
				var newParams, url = 'http' + (document.location.href.charAt(4) == 's' ? 's://sb' : '://b') + '.scorecardresearch.com/b?c1=2&c2=14366613';
				url += '&ns_site=master&mo_vs_pl=we&mo_vslabel=metro&mo_site=metro&mo_sitesection=MetroWeb&mo_domain=metro.co.uk&ns_type=view&';
				try {
					this.pageParams = this.getPageParams();
					newParams = this.jsonToQueryString(this.pageParams);
					this.udm_(url + newParams);
				} catch (exception) {
					var param2 = 'mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> trackPageView';
					this.udm_(url + param2);
				}
			},

			getPageParams: function (referrer, currentHost) {
				try {
					var referrer = referrer || document.referrer;
					var currentHost = currentHost || document.location.hostname;
					var params = {
						'mo_domain'      : document.location.hostname,
						'mo_page_name'   : this.getPageName(),
						'mo_channel'     : metro.pageData.topCategory,
						'mo_sub_channel' : metro.pageData.subCategory,
						'mo_content_type': metro.pageData.type,
						'mo_ref_do'      : this.getReferrerHost(),
						'mo_vs_ct'       : 'ge', // content type - default general
						'name'           : ''
					};

					// Pick up data left in cookie from any internal link click that might've brought us here
					var eventCookie = this.readCookie('metro-event-comscore');
					if (eventCookie) {
						var c = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(eventCookie));
						params.mo_lnk_pt = c.pageType; // Page Type
						// params.mo_lnk_mod = ''; // Module Name
						params.mo_lnk_link = c.track || ''; // Module Link
						// params.mo_lnk_more = ''; // More Details - data-track-destination, but we only use it in metro-thumbnail-link.php
						this.eraseCookie('metro-event-comscore');
					}

					this.initAdvancedPageParams(params, referrer, currentHost);
					return params;
				} catch (exception) {
					params = {
						'mo_err_msg': exception.message + ' ==> getPageParams'
					};
					return params;
				}
			},

			createCookie: function (name, value, days) {
				if (days) {
					var date = new Date();
					date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
					var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
				}
				else var expires = "";
				document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
			},

			readCookie: function (name) {
				var nameEQ = name + "=";
				var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
				for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
					var c = ca[i];
					while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
					if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
				}
				return null;
			},

			eraseCookie: function (name) {
				this.createCookie(name, "", -1);
			},

			/**
			 * Subscribe handler to internal click events. We set a cookie registering the event
			 * which we pick up on the next page load and report to comscore in getPageParams
			 * TODO - subscribe a similar handler to metro:event:click so we're recording clicks on elements without an internal href or with no href
			 */
			initClickTracking: function () {
				if (metro && metro.utils) {
					metro.utils.Observer('metro:event:link:internal').subscribe(function (track, el) {
						if (!metro.allCookies) {
							return;
						}
						metro.allCookies.removeItem('metro-event-comscore', '/');
						var cookieValue = {
							track   : track,
							pageType: metro.pageData.type
						};
						metro.allCookies.setItem('metro-event-comscore', JSON.stringify(cookieValue), null, '/');
					});
					metro.utils.Observer('metro:event:link:external').subscribe(function (track, el) {
						metro.comscore.trackLink('', track, el);
					});
					metro.utils.Observer('metro:event:click').subscribe(function (track, el) {
						metro.comscore.trackLink('', track, el);
					});
				}
			},

			trackLink: function (widgetName, linkName, linkEl) {
				var newParams, url = 'http' + (document.location.href.charAt(4) == 's' ? 's://sb' : '://b') + '.scorecardresearch.com/b?c1=22&c2=14366613';
				url += '&ns_site=master&mo_vs_pl=we&mo_vslabel=metro&mo_site=metro&mo_sitesection=MetroWeb&mo_domain=metro.co.uk&ns_type=hidden&';
				try {
					this.linkParams = this.getLinkParams(widgetName, linkName, linkEl);
					newParams = this.jsonToQueryString(this.linkParams);
					this.udm_(url + newParams);
				} catch (exception) {
					var param2 = 'mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> trackLink';
					this.udm_(url + param2);
				}
			},

			trackEvent: function (args) {
				// TODO:
			},

			getLinkParams: function (widgetName, linkName, linkEl) {
				try {
					var dataTrackDestination = null;
					var params = {
						'mo_domain'      : document.location.hostname,
						'mo_page_name'   : this.getPageName(),
						'mo_channel'     : metro.pageData.topCategory,
						'mo_sub_channel' : metro.pageData.subCategory,
						'mo_content_type': 'link_track',
						'mo_ref_do'      : this.getReferrerHost(),
						'mo_vs_ct'       : 'cl',
						'name'           : 'Metro.general.custom.link-click.event',
						'mo_lnk_pt'      : metro.pageData.type, // Page Type
						'mo_lnk_mod'     : widgetName || 'Not Available', // Module Name
						'mo_lnk_link'    : linkName || 'Not Available', // Module Link
						'mo_lnk_more'    : '' // More Details
					};
					if (linkEl) {
						params.mo_lnk_href = linkEl.href;
						dataTrackDestination = linkEl.getAttribute('data-track-destination');
					}
					if (dataTrackDestination !== null) {
						params.mo_lnk_more = dataTrackDestination;
					}
					return params;
				} catch (exception) {
					params = {
						'mo_err_msg': exception.message + ' ==> getLinkParams'
					};
					return params;
				}
			},

			jsonToQueryString: function (json) {
				var q = new Array();
				try {
					for (var property in json) {
						if (json.hasOwnProperty(property)) {
							q.push(encodeURIComponent(property) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(json[property]));
						}
					}
					return q.join('&');
				} catch (exception) {
					return ('mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> jsonToQueryString');
				}
			},

			getPageName: function () {
				var pageName = metro.pageData.requestUrl;
				if (pageName === '/') {
					pageName = 'home';
				}
				return pageName;
			},

			getReferrerHost: function () {
				try {
					var refererHost = "direct";
					if (document.referrer) {
						var docReferrerHostMatches = new RegExp("://([^/]*)/.*").exec(document.referrer);
						if (docReferrerHostMatches) {
							var docReferrerHost = docReferrerHostMatches[1];
							refererHost = docReferrerHost;
						}
					}
					return refererHost;
				} catch (exception) {
					return ('mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> getReferrerHost');
				}

			},

			/**
			 * @param referrer
			 * @returns {boolean}
			 */
			isEntryPage: function (referrer, currentHost) {
				if ((referrer === '') || (typeof referrer !== 'string')) {
					// Direct
					return true;
				} else if (referrer.indexOf(currentHost) === -1) {
					// From another site
					return true;
				}
				return false;
			},

			initAdvancedPageParams: function (params, referrer, currentHost) {
				try {
					if (this.isEntryPage(referrer, currentHost)) {
						params.mo_entry_page = metro.pageData.requestUrl;
					}
					if ((metro.pageData.type == 'article') || (metro.pageData.type === 'gallery')) {
						params.name = this.getComScoreName(metro.pageData.subCategory, 'article', metro.pageData.postId);
						params.mo_article_id = metro.pageData.postId;
						params.mo_article_title = metro.pageData.title;
						params.mo_article_author = metro.pageData.author;
						params.mo_ar_owner = metro.pageData.creator;
						params.mo_ar_age_hh = metro.pageData.postAge;
						params.mo_article_pd = this.getPubDate();
						params.mo_article_ph = this.getPubTime();
						params.mo_ar_age_dd = this.getAgeInDays(metro.pageData.pubDate, new Date());
						if (!params.mo_events) {
							params.mo_events = 'article_view';
						} else {
							params.mo_events = params.mo_events + ',article_view';
						}
						if (metro.pageData.isClubMetro === true) {
							params.mo_vs_ct = 'cm';
							params.mo_content_type = 'club metro blogs article';
						} else if (metro.pageData.isBlogPost === true) {
							params.mo_vs_ct = 'ba';
							params.mo_content_type = 'blogs article';
						} else {
							params.mo_vs_ct = 'ar';
						}
						if (metro.pageData.containsBrightcove) {
							params.mo_events += ',bc_videos';
						}
						if (metro.pageData.containsYoutube) {
							params.mo_events += ',yt_videos';
						}
					}
					if ((metro.pageData.type) && ((metro.pageData.type === 'home'))) {
						// Home page
						params.name = this.getComScoreName(metro.pageData.subCategory, 'home');
						params.mo_vs_ct = 'ho';
					}
					if ((metro.pageData.type) && ((metro.pageData.type.indexOf('catpage:') >= 0))) {
						// Channel or sub-channel page
						params.name = this.getComScoreName(metro.pageData.subCategory, 'home');
						params.mo_vs_ct = 'ch';
					}
					if ((metro.pageData.type) && ((metro.pageData.type === 'tag'))) {
						params.name = 'Metro.tags.' + this.getItemSlug(metro.pageData.requestUrl, '/tag/') + '.tag.page';
						params.mo_vs_ct = 'tp';
					}
					if ((metro.pageData.type) && ((metro.pageData.type === 'author'))) {
						params.name = 'Metro.authors.' + this.getItemSlug(metro.pageData.requestUrl, '/author/') + '.author.page';
						params.mo_vs_ct = 'au';
					}
					if ((metro.pageData.type) && ((metro.pageData.type === 'errorPage'))) {
						params.name = 'Metro.home.default.error.page';
						params.mo_vs_ct = 'er';
						params.mo_content_type = 'error';
					}
				}
				catch (exception) {
					return (params.mo_err_msg = exception.message + ' ==> initAdvancedPageParams');
				}
			},

			/**
			 * comScore page name string
			 * @param subChannel e.g. "sport/football"
			 * @param pageType e.g. "article"
			 * @return e.g.
			 Metro.home.default.home.page
			 Metro.news.default.home.page
			 Metro.news.uk.home.page
			 Metro.news.uk.article.5094372.page
			 Metro.news.world.home.page
			 Metro.sport.default.home.page
			 Metro.sport.oddballs.home.page
			 Metro.sport.football.home.page
			 Metro.tags.one-direction.tag.page
			 Metro.home.default.error.page
			 */
			getComScoreName: function (subChannel, pageType, postId) {
				var subChannelStr = "home.default";
				if (subChannel) {
					subChannelStr = (subChannel.indexOf("/") < 0) ? subChannel + ".default" : subChannel;
				}
				var postIdStr = (postId) ? "." + postId : '';
				var shortName = "Metro." + subChannelStr.replace('/', '.') + "." + pageType + postIdStr;
				return shortName + ".page";
			},

			/**
			 * Strips prefixes like /tag/ and /author/ from request URL slug
			 * @param requestUrl /tag/one-direction/
			 * @param prefix like /tag/
			 * @returns {string}
			 */
			getItemSlug: function (requestUrl, prefix) {
				// Tag page Metro.tags.one-direction.tag.page
				var prefixLen = prefix.length;
				var targetLength = requestUrl.length - (prefixLen + '/'.length);
				var slug = requestUrl.substr(prefixLen, targetLength);
				return slug;
			},


			getPubDate: function () {
				try {
					var tmpDate = metro.pageData.pubDate.split("-");
					pubDate = tmpDate[2] + tmpDate[1] + tmpDate[0];
					return pubDate;
				}
				catch (exception) {
					return ('mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> getPubDate');
				}
			},

			getPubTime: function () {
				try {
					var tmpTime = metro.pageData.pubTime.split(":");
					return tmpTime[0];
				}
				catch (exception) {
					return ('mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> getPubTime');
				}
			},

			/* @param pubDateCalendarDate e.g. metro.pageData.pubDate
			 * @param currentDate e.g. new Date()
			 */
			getAgeInDays: function (pubDateCalendarDate, currentDate) {
				try {
					var one_day = 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24;
					var pubDateArray = pubDateCalendarDate.split("-");
					var pubDateObj = new Date(pubDateArray[2], (pubDateArray[1] - 1), pubDateArray[0]);
					var ageInDays = Math.ceil((currentDate.getTime() - pubDateObj.getTime()) / (one_day));
					return ageInDays;
				}
				catch (exception) {
					return ('mo_err_msg=' + exception.message + ' ==> getAgeInDays');
				}
			}

		}

		metro.comscore.trackPageView();

	})(metro, window);

	if(jQuery) {
		jQuery(metro.comscore.initClickTracking);
	}

</script>

	// Load deferred scripts
	metro.deferredScripts = metro.deferredScripts || [];

	// Twitter
	metro.deferredScripts.push({
		url: '//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js',
		id: 'twitter-widgets',
		callback: function () {
			// Stop Twitter widgets.js from taking over the function of the top Twitter button
			jQuery('.shrb-top.twitter').attr({
				href: '#'
			});
			jQuery(document).on('click', '.share-button.twitter', metro.share.sharePageToTwitter);
		}
	});

		metro.deferredScripts.push({
		url: 'https://web.btncdn.com/v1/button.js',
		id: 'usebutton'
	});

		url: 'https://assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
		id: 'pinterest-embeds'
	});
	
	(function (metro) {

		function loadScripts() {
			if (metro.deferredScripts.length > 0) {
				for (var i = 0; i < metro.deferredScripts.length; i++) {
					loadScript(metro.deferredScripts[i]);
				}
			}
			window.removeEventListener('metro:scroll', loadScripts);
			window.removeEventListener('load', loadScripts);
		}

		function loadScript(obj) {
			if (document.getElementById(obj.id)) {
				return;
			}
			var script = document.createElement('script');
			script.src = obj.url;
			script.id = obj.id;
			document.head.appendChild(script);
			if ('function' === typeof obj.callback) {
				obj.callback();
			}
		}

		if ('article' === metro.pageData.type) {
			window.addEventListener('metro:scroll', loadScripts);
		} else {
			window.addEventListener('load', loadScripts);
		}

	})(metro);

</script>
